\DoxyCodeLine{55 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{56     CD3DX12\_VIEWPORT() = \textcolor{keywordflow}{default};}

\DoxyCodeLine{58         D3D12\_VIEWPORT( o )}
\DoxyCodeLine{59     \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{60     \textcolor{keyword}{explicit} CD3DX12\_VIEWPORT(}
\DoxyCodeLine{61         FLOAT topLeftX,}
\DoxyCodeLine{62         FLOAT topLeftY,}
\DoxyCodeLine{63         FLOAT width,}
\DoxyCodeLine{64         FLOAT height,}
\DoxyCodeLine{65         FLOAT minDepth = D3D12\_MIN\_DEPTH,}
\DoxyCodeLine{66         FLOAT maxDepth = D3D12\_MAX\_DEPTH ) \textcolor{keyword}{noexcept}}
\DoxyCodeLine{67     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{68         TopLeftX = topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{69         TopLeftY = topLeftY;}
\DoxyCodeLine{70         Width = width;}
\DoxyCodeLine{71         Height = height;}
\DoxyCodeLine{72         MinDepth = minDepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{73         MaxDepth = maxDepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{74     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{75     \textcolor{keyword}{explicit} CD3DX12\_VIEWPORT(}
\DoxyCodeLine{76         \_In\_ ID3D12Resource* pResource,}
\DoxyCodeLine{77         UINT mipSlice = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{78         FLOAT topLeftX = 0.0f,}
\DoxyCodeLine{79         FLOAT topLeftY = 0.0f,}
\DoxyCodeLine{80         FLOAT minDepth = D3D12\_MIN\_DEPTH,}
\DoxyCodeLine{81         FLOAT maxDepth = D3D12\_MAX\_DEPTH ) \textcolor{keyword}{noexcept}}
\DoxyCodeLine{82     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{83         \textcolor{keyword}{auto} Desc = pResource-\/>GetDesc();}
\DoxyCodeLine{84         \textcolor{keyword}{const} UINT64 SubresourceWidth = Desc.Width >> mipSlice;}
\DoxyCodeLine{85         \textcolor{keyword}{const} UINT64 SubresourceHeight = Desc.Height >> mipSlice;}
\DoxyCodeLine{86         \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (Desc.Dimension)}
\DoxyCodeLine{87         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{88         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} D3D12\_RESOURCE\_DIMENSION\_BUFFER:}
\DoxyCodeLine{89             TopLeftX = topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{90             TopLeftY = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{91             Width = float(Desc.Width) -\/ topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{92             Height = 1.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{93             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{94         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} D3D12\_RESOURCE\_DIMENSION\_TEXTURE1D:}
\DoxyCodeLine{95             TopLeftX = topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{96             TopLeftY = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{97             Width = (SubresourceWidth ? float(SubresourceWidth) : 1.0f) -\/ topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{98             Height = 1.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{99             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{100         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} D3D12\_RESOURCE\_DIMENSION\_TEXTURE2D:}
\DoxyCodeLine{101         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} D3D12\_RESOURCE\_DIMENSION\_TEXTURE3D:}
\DoxyCodeLine{102             TopLeftX = topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{103             TopLeftY = topLeftY;}
\DoxyCodeLine{104             Width = (SubresourceWidth ? float(SubresourceWidth) : 1.0f) -\/ topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{105             Height = (SubresourceHeight ? float(SubresourceHeight) : 1.0f) -\/ topLeftY;}
\DoxyCodeLine{106             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{107         \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{108         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{109 }
\DoxyCodeLine{110         MinDepth = minDepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{111         MaxDepth = maxDepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{112     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{113 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{3271 \textcolor{comment}{//================================================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3272 \textcolor{comment}{// D3DX12 State Object Creation Helpers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3273 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3274 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper classes for creating new style state objects out of an arbitrary set of subobjects.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3275 \textcolor{comment}{// Uses STL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3276 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3277 \textcolor{comment}{// Start by instantiating CD3DX12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_DESC (see it's public methods).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3278 \textcolor{comment}{// One of its methods is CreateSubobject(), which has a comment showing a couple of options for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3279 \textcolor{comment}{// defining subobjects using the helper classes for each subobject (CD3DX12\_DXIL\_LIBRARY\_SUBOBJECT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3280 \textcolor{comment}{// etc.). The subobject helpers each have methods specific to the subobject for configuring it's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3281 \textcolor{comment}{// contents.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3282 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3283 \textcolor{comment}{//================================================================================================}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3323         \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{3331         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3332             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_SubobjectArray[i].Type == D3D12\_STATE\_SUBOBJECT\_TYPE\_SUBOBJECT\_TO\_EXPORTS\_ASSOCIATION)}

\DoxyCodeLine{3354     \textcolor{comment}{// CreateSubobject creates a sububject helper (e.g. CD3DX12\_HIT\_GROUP\_SUBOBJECT)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3355     \textcolor{comment}{// whose lifetime is owned by this class.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3356     \textcolor{comment}{// e.g.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3357     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3358     \textcolor{comment}{//    CD3DX12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_DESC Collection1(D3D12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_TYPE\_COLLECTION);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3359     \textcolor{comment}{//    auto Lib0 = Collection1.CreateSubobject<CD3DX12\_DXIL\_LIBRARY\_SUBOBJECT>();}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3360     \textcolor{comment}{//    Lib0-\/>SetDXILLibrary(\&pMyAppDxilLibs[0]);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3361     \textcolor{comment}{//    Lib0-\/>DefineExport(L"{}rayGenShader0"{}); // in practice these export listings might be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3362     \textcolor{comment}{//                                          // data/engine driven}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3363     \textcolor{comment}{//    etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3364     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3365     \textcolor{comment}{// Alternatively, users can instantiate sububject helpers explicitly, such as via local}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3366     \textcolor{comment}{// variables instead, passing the state object desc that should point to it into the helper}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3367     \textcolor{comment}{// constructor (or call mySubobjectHelper.AddToStateObject(Collection1)).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3368     \textcolor{comment}{// In this alternative scenario, the user must keep the subobject alive as long as the state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3369     \textcolor{comment}{// object it is associated with is alive, else it's pointer references will be stale.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3370     \textcolor{comment}{// e.g.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3371     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3372     \textcolor{comment}{//    CD3DX12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_DESC RaytracingState2(D3D12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_TYPE\_RAYTRACING\_PIPELINE);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3373     \textcolor{comment}{//    CD3DX12\_DXIL\_LIBRARY\_SUBOBJECT LibA(RaytracingState2);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3374     \textcolor{comment}{//    LibA.SetDXILLibrary(\&pMyAppDxilLibs[4]); // not manually specifying exports}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3375     \textcolor{comment}{//                                             // -\/ meaning all exports in the libraries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3376     \textcolor{comment}{//                                             // are exported}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3377     \textcolor{comment}{//    etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3378 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3379     \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
